padding:0 15px;">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\n<div class="paragraph"><u><strong><font color="#508d24">GREEN BUILDING</font></strong></u><br /><br /><font color="#2a2a2a">We are proud to inform our customers that </font><strong><font color="#508d24">BETA Engineering has achieved the status of BRONZE CERTIFIED&nbsp;from the&nbsp;ARZ Building Rating System (From LGBC).</font><br />&#8203;</strong><br /><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51)"><span><span>The&nbsp;<span><strong>ARZ BRS</strong></span>&nbsp;is an evidence based approach to assessing how green a building is. The system includes a list of technologies, techniques, procedures and energy consumption levels that LGBC expects to see in green buildings. An assessor accredited by LGBC will take an&nbsp;<strong>inventory of the energy and water consumption, technologies, techniques and procedures</strong>&nbsp;that are used in the building and then LGBC will score the building according to how well the inventory matches the list of technologies, techniques and procedures that make up the ARZ BRS requirements. The results of an assessment are a certificate issued by LGBC that details the level achieved, an accompanying&nbsp;<strong><span>report with recommendations</span></strong>&nbsp;on how the rating level could be improved and a plaque to be erected on the building premises.</span></span></span><br />&nbsp;<br /><span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51)"><span><span>Green building rating systems measure how effectively sustainable construction, management, and operations of buildings blend into their environments. Green building principles require a long term view, taking into account a building&rsquo;s environmental impact throughout its life. It should include all stages from the design and construction of a building through to its use, demolition and finally the recycling or disposal of the building materials. Studies have shown that green rated buildings all around the world tend to:</span></span></span><br />&nbsp;<br />&#9658;<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51)"><span><span>Have lower operating costs for building owner</span></span></span><br />&#9658;<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51)"><span><span>Protect owners and tenants from higher utility costs</span></span></span><br />&#9658;<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51)"><span><span>Increase worker productivity by affording them a healthier working environment</span></span></span><br />&#9658;<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51)"><span><span>Demonstrate a company&rsquo;s corporate social responsibility</span></span></span><br />&#9658;<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51)"><span><span>Command higher rents</span></span></span><br />&#9658;<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51)"><span><span>Attract higher volumes of clients seeking to do business there</span></span></span><br />&#9658;<span style="color:rgb(51, 51, 51)"><span><span>Carry a sense of prestige</span></span></span></div>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t</td>\t\t\t\t<td class="wsite-multicol-col" style="width:34.631578947368%; is a national financing mechanism initiated by the Central Bank of Lebanon (Banque du Liban-BDL) dedicated to the financing of green energy projects in Lebanon.<br />&nbsp;<br /><strong><font color="#508d24">NEEREA</font></strong> is a national platform built and launched on 25 November 2010 based on the Circular 236 of the Central Bank of Lebanon (BDL), which, in collaboration with the European Union (EU) lists the terms and conditions to get subsidized green loans. In 2013, as per circular 313, 318, and lately 346, BDL introduced new incentives to focus on energy efficiency, renewable energy and&nbsp;certified green buildings.<br />&nbsp;<br /><strong><font color="#508d24">NEEREA is a green financing </font></strong>mechanism that provides interest-free long-term loans to residential, commercial, non-profit and industrial users for all energy efficiency and renewable energy projects for new and existing facilities. The loan is eligible for new environmental friendly projects or for existing projects to enhance their conditions in order to become environmentally sound. The loan has a ceiling of 20 million USD and is offered at an interest rate of 0.6% for period that should not exceed 14 years including a grace period of 6 months to 4 years. The green loans are provided through all the Lebanese commercial banks to directly reach the end user.<br />&nbsp;<br />NEEREA also includes a grant scheme based on an agreement signed between the BDL and the European Union (EU).<br />&nbsp;<br />In addition to the BDL financing tools, the technical support and capacity building activities are done by the Lebanese Center for Energy Conservation (LCEC) to develop the know-how among all players. These activities are part of the contract signed between the BDL and the LCEC under the name "Technical Support Consultancy Services Agreement in Energy Efficiency and Renewable Energy".&nbsp;</font><br /><br /><br /></div>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t</td>\t\t\t\t<td class="wsite-multicol-col" style="width:49.359720605355%; padding:0 15px;">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\n<div
